Work Sans Regular (WorkSans[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'WorkSans-Regular', Everything looks good.

Work Sans Italic (WorkSans-Italic[wght].ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'WorkSans-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Please verify agains spec. It might be ok if it's a symbol font.
